    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e.role_id = @roleId_Value AND (lower(e.employee_name) LIKE @ToLower_contains OR lower(e.email) LIKE @ToLower_contains0)
    ORDER BY e.employee_id
    LIMIT @p4 OFFSET @p
) AS e0
INNER JOIN roles AS r ON e0.role_id = r.role_id
LEFT JOIN departments AS d ON e0.department_id = d.department_id
ORDER BY e0.employee_id
